<script>/*<![CDATA[*/ 

    // GPP Helper Function
    __tnt.ads.dfp.getGppData = function(callback) {
        var maxRetries = 5;
        var retryDelay = 400;
        var existsRetryCount = 0;
        var readyRetryCount = 0;
        var debug = /[?&]ads_log/.test(window.location.search);
        
        function checkGppExists() {
            if (typeof __gpp !== 'function') {
                existsRetryCount++;
                if (existsRetryCount < maxRetries) {
                    if (debug) console.log('GPP CMP not available, retrying... (' + existsRetryCount + '/' + maxRetries + ')');
                    setTimeout(checkGppExists, retryDelay);
                    return;
                } else {
                    if (debug) console.log('GPP CMP not available after ' + maxRetries + ' attempts');
                    callback(null);
                    return;
                }
            }
            fetchGppData();
        }
        
        function fetchGppData() {
            try {
                __gpp('ping', function(pingData, success) {
                    if (!success || pingData.signalStatus !== 'ready') {
                        readyRetryCount++;
                        if (readyRetryCount < maxRetries) {
                            if (debug) console.log('GPP signal not ready, retrying... (' + readyRetryCount + '/' + maxRetries + ')');
                            setTimeout(fetchGppData, retryDelay);
                            return;
                        } else {
                            if (debug) console.log('GPP signal not ready after ' + maxRetries + ' attempts');
                            callback(pingData || null);
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    callback(pingData);
                });
            } catch (error) {
                if (debug) console.log('Error getting GPP data: ' + error.message);
                callback(null);
            }
        }
        
        checkGppExists();
    };

    // Apply GPP Privacy Settings
    __tnt.ads.dfp.setPrivacySettings = function(callback) {
        __tnt.ads.dfp.getGppData(function(gppData) {
            googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                var disableTargetedAds = false;
                var debug = /[?&]ads_log/.test(window.location.search);
        
                if (gppData && gppData.parsedSections) {
                    for (var sectionName in gppData.parsedSections) {
                        var sectionData = gppData.parsedSections[sectionName];
                        if (!sectionData) continue;
                        
                        var section = sectionData[Object.keys(sectionData)[0]];
                        if (!section) continue;

                        // GDPR (tcfeuv2) - Check Purpose 4
                        if (sectionName === 'tcfeuv2') {
                            var purposes = section.Purpose && section.Purpose.Consent;
                            if (!purposes || !purposes[3]) {
                                disableTargetedAds = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }

                        // Canada (tcfcav1) - Check Purpose 4
                        if (sectionName === 'tcfcav1') {
                            var purposes = section.PurposesExpressConsent;
                            if (!purposes || !purposes[3]) {
                                disableTargetedAds = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }

                        // CCPA (uspv1) - Check opt-out of sale
                        if (sectionName === 'uspv1') {
                            var uspString = section.uspString || '';
                            if (uspString[2] === 'Y') {
                                disableTargetedAds = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }

                        // US National & States - Check opt-out flags
                        var usRegex = /^(usnat|usca|usva|usco|usut|usct|usfl|usmt|usor|ustx|usde|usia|usne|usnh|usnj|ustn)$/i;
                        if (usRegex.test(sectionName)) {
                            if (section.TargetedAdvertisingOptOut === 1 || 
                                section.SaleOptOut === 1 || 
                                section.SharingOptOut === 1) {
                                disableTargetedAds = true;
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    if (debug) console.log('Disable Targeted Ads: ' + disableTargetedAds);
                } else {
                    if (debug) console.log('No GPP data available, using default privacy settings');
                }
                
                // Set privacy settings in GPT
                googletag.pubads().setPrivacySettings({
                    'restrictDataProcessing': disableTargetedAds
                });
                
                if (callback) callback();
            });
        });
    };

    // Main initialization with GPP check
    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
    
        // Targeting for client browser
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('browser', __tnt.client.browser.name);
        
        // Targeting for schain
        // Targeting for keywords
        if (__tnt.ads.dfp.targeting) {
            for (var k in __tnt.ads.dfp.targeting) {
                if (__tnt.ads.dfp.targeting.hasOwnProperty(k)) {
                    googletag.pubads().setTargeting(k,__tnt.ads.dfp.targeting[k]);
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Viewable impression event listener
            googletag.pubads().addEventListener('impressionViewable', function(event) {
                for (var key in gptAdSlots) {
                    if (gptAdSlots[key] === event.slot && __tnt.ads.slots[key]) {
                        if (!__tnt.ads.slots[key].viewableImpression) __tnt.ads.slots[key].viewableImpression = true;
                    }
                }
            });

        // Publisher provided ID(PPID)
        if (window.localStorage) {
            var sID = window.localStorage.getItem('_us_master_id');
            if (sID) {
                if (window.dataLayer) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'tncms.ad.userstitch_id': sID
                    });
                }
                googletag.pubads().setPublisherProvidedId(sID);
            }
        }
        
        // Disable initial ad load for all ad variants
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
        
        // Fetch multiple ads at the same time
        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        
        // Enable all GPT services for all defined ad slots
        googletag.enableServices();
    });
 /*]]>*/</script>

async function handleCreditCardUpdateAccess(accountNumber) {
  try {
  
  
    if (window.location.pathname.includes("/update_credit_card")) {
    return;
    }
  
    const subscription = await getSubscriptionForCreditCardUpdate(accountNumber);
    
 

    if (!subscription) {
      return;
    }

  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Error getting subscription for credit card update:", error);
  }
}



async function getSubscriptionForCreditCardUpdate(accountNumber) {
 

  const response = await authenticatedFetch(
    `https://auth.nola.com/api/v1/auth0Protected/prod/checkAccess`,
    {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify({
        accountNumber: accountNumber,
        dialogue: true,
  }),
    }
  );



  let data;

  try {
    data = await response.json();
  } catch (error) {
    data = await response.text();
  }



  if (!response.ok) {
    return false;
  }
  
  if(data.sendEventToBlueconic) {
  blueConicClient.createEvent("update_credit_card_event");
  }
   

  return data;
}


const AuthService = (() => {
  let clientPromise = null;
  let scriptPromise = null;

  function loadAuth0Script() {
    if (window.auth0?.createAuth0Client) {
      return Promise.resolve();
    }

    if (!scriptPromise) {
      scriptPromise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const script = document.createElement("script");

        script.src =
          "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@auth0/auth0-spa-js@2.0.4/dist/auth0-spa-js.production.js";

        script.async = true;
        script.crossOrigin = "anonymous";

        script.onload = resolve;
        script.onerror = () => reject(new Error("Auth0 script failed to load"));

        document.head.appendChild(script);
      });
    }

    return scriptPromise;
  }

  async function getClient() {
    await loadAuth0Script();

    if (!clientPromise) {
      clientPromise = window.auth0.createAuth0Client({
        domain: "login.nola.com",
        clientId: "NaH6oNwKnnx6ygH27LTPY1PApkRdNTJU",
        authorizationParams: {
          redirect_uri:
            "https://www.nola.com/auth0-redirect",
        },
      });
    }

    return clientPromise;
  }

  async function getIdToken() {
    try {
     

      const client = await getClient();

      await client.getTokenSilently();

      const claims = await client.getIdTokenClaims();

      return claims?.__raw || null;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("getIdToken failed:", error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  async function isLoggedIn() {
    const token = await getIdToken();
    
    return !!token;
  }

  return {
    getIdToken,
    isLoggedIn,
  };
})();

async function authenticatedFetch(url, options = {}) {
  const token = await AuthService.getIdToken();

  if (!token) {
    throw new Error("User is not authenticated");
  }

  return fetch(url, {
    ...options,
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json",
      ...(options.headers || {}),
      Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
    },
  });
}         

</script>

        function styleMobileNavBar(navigaEvent) {
            
            const eventData = navigaEvent.detail
            let firstName;
            
            const AuthProfileGivenName = eventData.EventData?.AuthProfile?.given_name; 
            const DigitalAccessSubscriptionFirstName = eventData.EventData?.MG2AccountData?.DigitalAccess?.Subscription?.FirstName;
            
            if(AuthProfileGivenName) { 
                firstName = AuthProfileGivenName 
            }
            if (DigitalAccessSubscriptionFirstName) { 
                firstName = `${DigitalAccessSubscriptionFirstName[0]}${DigitalAccessSubscriptionFirstName.slice(1).toLowerCase()}`
            } 
              
            const greeting = firstName && firstName != '' ? `Hi, ${firstName}!` : "Hi there!"
            
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $("#nav-user-firstName").html(greeting);
                $(".nav-signIn-container").css({ visibility: "hidden" });
                $(".nav-account-container").css({ visibility: "visible" });
                $(".open-setting-container").css({ visibility: "visible" });
            })
            
            document.removeEventListener("onAuthorized", styleMobileNavBar);
            document.removeEventListener("onHasAccess", styleMobileNavBar);
            document.removeEventListener("onHasNoActiveSubscription", styleMobileNavBar);
        }

(function () {
  // console.log("jw event tracking v2");

  // ─── GA4 helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  // GA4 event names must be snake_case, ≤40 chars, no dots or capitals.
  // e.g. 'firstFrame' → 'first_frame', 'adImpression' → 'ad_impression'
  function toSnakeCase(str) {
    return str.replace(/([A-Z])/g, "_$1").toLowerCase();
  }

  // ─── Shared listener attachment ────────────────────────────────────────────
  function attachListeners(player, elementId) {
    [
      "play",
      //"pause",
      "complete",
      "firstFrame",
      //"adImpression",
      //"adComplete",
      "error",
    ].forEach((evt) => {
      player.on(evt, (data) => {
        const item = player.getPlaylistItem() || {};
        //console.log("evt", data, item);

        const eventPayload = {
          jw_event: evt,
          media_id: item.mediaid ?? null,
          media_title: item.title ?? null,
          element_id: elementId ?? null,
          media_tags: item.tags ?? null,
          media_playlist: item.feedid ?? null,
          //media_duration: player.getDuration?.() ?? null,
          //media_position: player.getPosition?.() ?? null,
          page_location: window.location.href,
          page_title: document.title,
        };

        window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

        window.dataLayer.push({
          event: "jw_player_" + toSnakeCase(evt),
          ...eventPayload,
        });

        // console.log("jw evt", evt, eventPayload);
      });
    });
  }

  // ─── Core patching logic ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function patchJWPlayer() {
    const origJW = window.jwplayer;

    // Retroactively instrument players that are already set up.
    // JW stamps the '.jwplayer' class on the container when setup() completes —
    // far more reliable than integer-index enumeration.
    document.querySelectorAll(".jwplayer[id]").forEach((el) => {
      const player = origJW(el.id);
      if (player && !player.__myHooked) {
        attachListeners(player, el.id);
        player.__myHooked = true;
      }
    });

    // Patch window.jwplayer to instrument all future players.
    window.jwplayer = function () {
      const instance = origJW.apply(this, arguments);
      const elementId =
        typeof arguments[0] === "string" ? arguments[0] : arguments[0]?.id;

      if (!instance.__myHooked) {
        const origSetup = instance.setup.bind(instance);
        instance.setup = function (config) {
          const player = origSetup(config);
          attachListeners(player, elementId);
          return player;
        };
        instance.__myHooked = true;
      }
      return instance;
    };

    // Preserve all static properties and prototype so nothing downstream breaks.
    Object.keys(origJW).forEach((k) => {
      window.jwplayer[k] = origJW[k];
    });
    window.jwplayer.prototype = origJW.prototype;
  }

  // ─── Entry point ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  // Poll until window.jwplayer is available (handles async script loading),
  // then patch immediately. If it's already present, the interval fires once
  // on the next tick and clears itself.
  const waitForJW = setInterval(() => {
    if (!window.jwplayer) return;
    clearInterval(waitForJW);
    patchJWPlayer();
  }, 50);
})();

</script>

      <script>
        function getAndDeleteCookies(cookieWord) {
           //const cDecoded = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie); //to be careful
           const cDecoded = document.cookie;
           const cookiesArr = cDecoded.split('; ');
           const foundCookies = cookiesArr.filter((cookie) => cookie.includes(cookieWord)).map((word) => word.split("=")[0])
             return foundCookies.forEach((cookieName) =>  {
              let pathUrl = cookieName.split("/")[1];
           // let cookieNameClean = cookieName.replace(/\//g, "%2F");
            let cookieNameClean = cookieName
         document.cookie = `${cookieNameClean}=;path=/${pathUrl};expires=${new Date(0).toUTCString()}`
             document.cookie = `${cookieNameClean}=;path=/;expires=${new Date(0).toUTCString()}`
        }) 
       }
       
       getAndDeleteCookies("scroll@");
        </script>

            $(function(){
                var bloxServiceIDs = [];
                var bloxUserServiceIds = [];
                var dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

                
                bloxServiceIDs.push();
                

                if (__tnt.user.services){
                    var bloxUserServiceIDs = __tnt.user.services.replace('%2C',',').split(',');
                }

                // GTM tncms.subscription.paid_access_service_ids
                if(bloxServiceIDs){
                    dataLayer.push({'tncms':{'subscription':{'access_service_ids':bloxServiceIDs.toString()}}});
                }

                // GTM tncms.subscrption.user_service_ids
                if(bloxUserServiceIDs){
                    dataLayer.push({'tncms':{'subscription':{'user_service_ids':bloxUserServiceIDs.toString()}}});
                }
            });

      requestUrlNavButtonMobile,
    );

    /** END */

    let mobileUrl = `https://subscribe.nola.com/digitalplan?ofrgp_id=531&g2i_source=subscribebuttonmn&requestUrl=${encodedRequestUrlNavButtonMobile}`;

    let mobileSubscribeButtonText = "Subscribe for $1";

    let nowWidthLogin = window.innerWidth;

    let desktopNavbar = document.querySelector(".desktop-navbar");

    accountContainerDiv.setAttribute("id", "nav-account-container");
    accountContainerDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-account-container");

    accountNameAndSvgContainer.setAttribute(
      "class",
      "nav-name-and-svg-container",
    );

    accountNameContainerDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-name-container");

    formattedNameP.setAttribute("class", "nav-user-firstName");

    // formattedNameP.innerHTML =`Hello, ${formattedName}!`;

    accountIconUserDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-icon-user-container");

    checkWidthToIconUser(992, accountIconUserDiv);

    accountContainerDiv.appendChild(accountIconUserDiv);

    // Append the right children element to parent
    checkWidthToAppend(992, navbarHeader, desktopNavbar, accountContainerDiv);

    /* OPEN SETTINGS BLOCK */

    let openSettingsContainerDiv = document.createElement("div");
    openSettingsContainerDiv.setAttribute("class", "open-setting-container");

    const settings = [
      {
        name: "MY ACCOUNT",
        url: '<a href="https://myaccount.nola.com/" target="_blank"  class="MG2MyAccount"><strong>MY ACCOUNT',
        onclick: () => close(),
      },
      {
        name: "E-Edition",
        url: '<a href="https://app.nola.com/t/storefront/times_picayune" target="_blank"><strong>VIEW E-EDITION',
        onclick: () => close(),

        name: "LOG OUT",
        url: '<a href="#" class="MG2logout" data-mg2-action="logout"><strong>LOG OUT',
        onclick: () => close(),
      },

    let settingsDiv = document.createElement("div");
    settingsDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-settings-div");

    let settingsUl = document.createElement("ul");
    settingsUl.setAttribute("class", "nav-settings-ul");

    settingsDiv.appendChild(settingsUl);

    settings.map((setting) => {
      let settingLi = document.createElement("li");
      settingLi.setAttribute("class", "nav-setting-li");

      if (setting.onclick) {
        settingLi.onclick = setting.onclick;
      }

      settingLi.innerHTML = setting.url;
      settingsUl.appendChild(settingLi);
    });

    openSettingsContainerDiv.appendChild(settingsDiv);
    
    checkWidthToAppend(
      992,
      navbarHeader,
      desktopNavbar,
      openSettingsContainerDiv,
    );

    if (nowWidthLogin > 992) {
      accountContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseover", mouseOver);
      accountContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseout", mouseOut);

      openSettingsContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseover", mouseOver);
      openSettingsContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseout", mouseOut);
    } else {
      accountContainerDiv.removeEventListener("mouseover", mouseOver);
      accountContainerDiv.removeEventListener("mouseout", mouseOut);
      let open = false;
      openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "0";
      settingsDiv.style.display = "none";
      accountContainerDiv.addEventListener("click", () => {
        if (!open) {
          open = !open;
          openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "80px";
          settingsDiv.style.display = "block";
        } else {
          open = !open;
          openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "0";
          settingsDiv.style.display = "none";
        }
      });
    }

    window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
      var width = window.innerWidth;

      if (width < 992) {
        accountContainerDiv.style.backgroundColor = "transparent";
        accountContainerDiv.removeEventListener("mouseover", mouseOver);
        accountContainerDiv.removeEventListener("mouseout", mouseOut);

        let open = false;
        accountContainerDiv.addEventListener("click", () => {
          if (!open) {
            open = !open;

            openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "80px";
            settingsDiv.style.display = "block";
          } else {
            open = !open;
            openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "0";
            settingsDiv.style.display = "none";
          }
        });
      } else {
        accountContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseover", mouseOver);
        accountContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseout", mouseOut);
        openSettingsContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseover", mouseOver);
        openSettingsContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseout", mouseOut);
      }
    });

    /* SIGN IN */

    let signInContainerDiv = document.createElement("div");
    signInContainerDiv.setAttribute("id", "nav-signIn-container");
    signInContainerDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-signIn-container");
    signInContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");

    let signInNameAndSvgContainer = document.createElement("div");
    signInNameAndSvgContainer.setAttribute(
      "class",
      "nav-name-and-svg-container",
    );

    signInContainerDiv.appendChild(signInNameAndSvgContainer);

    signInContainerDiv.style.border = "1px solid transparent";
    //signInContainerDiv.style.border = "1px solid #bbbbbb";
    // HERE

    let signInNameContainerDiv = document.createElement("div");
    signInNameContainerDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-name-container");

    let formattedSignInP = document.createElement("p");
    formattedSignInP.setAttribute("class", "nav-user-firstName");

    formattedSignInP.innerHTML =
      '<a id="signIn-Name-Login" href="#" class="MG2login" data-mg2-action="login">LOG IN';

    if (nowWidthLogin > 992) {
      signInContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseover", signInMouseOver);
      signInContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseout", signInMouseOut);
    }

    window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
      var width = window.innerWidth;

      if (width > 992) {
        signInContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseover", signInMouseOver);
        signInContainerDiv.addEventListener("mouseout", signInMouseOut);
      }
    });

    signInNameContainerDiv.appendChild(formattedSignInP);

    signInNameAndSvgContainer.appendChild(signInNameContainerDiv);

    let signInSvgContainerDiv = document.createElement("div");
    signInSvgContainerDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-svg-container");
    signInSvgContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");

    checkWidthToIconArrow(992, signInSvgContainerDiv);

    signInNameAndSvgContainer.appendChild(signInSvgContainerDiv);

    let signInUserIconContainer = document.createElement("div");
    signInUserIconContainer.setAttribute("id", "user_icon_container");

    signInUserIconContainer.innerHTML = `<a href="#" style="display:none" class="MG2login" data-mg2-action="login"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="${21}" height="${21}" fill="currentColor" class="bi bi-person-circle" viewBox="0 0 16 16">

  `;

    signInContainerDiv.appendChild(signInUserIconContainer);

    let signInIconUserDiv = document.createElement("div");
    signInIconUserDiv.setAttribute("id", "signin-nav-icon-user-container");
    signInIconUserDiv.setAttribute("class", "nav-icon-user-container");
    signInIconUserDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "login");

    checkWidthToIconUser(992, signInIconUserDiv);

    if (nowWidthLogin > 992) {
      formattedSignInP.innerHTML =
        '<a id="signIn-Name-Login" href="#" class="MG2login" data-mg2-action="login">LOG IN';
    } else {
      signInContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");
      signInSvgContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");
      signInIconUserDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");
      signInSvgContainerDiv.innerHTML = "";
      signInIconUserDiv.innerHTML = "";
      formattedSignInP.innerHTML = `<a href="${mobileUrl}" class="MG2Subscribe" data-mg2-action="subscribe"><button type="button" class="btn btn-default btn-sm log-in-button" style="background:#e44ab0; border-color:#000; color:#000;">${mobileSubscribeButtonText}`;

      } else {

        signInSvgContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");

        signInSvgContainerDiv.innerHTML = "";
        signInIconUserDiv.innerHTML = "";
        formattedSignInP.innerHTML = `<a href="${mobileUrl}" class="MG2Subscribe" data-mg2-action="subscribe"><button type="button" class="btn btn-default btn-sm log-in-button" style="background:#e44ab0; border-color:#000; color:#000;">${mobileSubscribeButtonText}`;
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("MG2logout").addEventListener("click", function () {
      if (nowWidthLogin < 992) {
        signInContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");
        signInSvgContainerDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");
        signInIconUserDiv.setAttribute("data-mg2-action", "subscribe");
        signInSvgContainerDiv.innerHTML = "";
        signInIconUserDiv.innerHTML = "";
        formattedSignInP.innerHTML = `<a href="${mobileUrl}" class="MG2Subscribe" data-mg2-action="subscribe"><button type="button" class="btn btn-default btn-sm log-in-button" style="background:#e44ab0; border-color:#000; color:#000;">${mobileSubscribeButtonText}`;
      }
    });

    signInContainerDiv.appendChild(signInIconUserDiv);

    checkWidthToAppend(992, navbarHeader, desktopNavbar, signInContainerDiv);

    // navbarHeader.appendChild(signInContainerDiv);

    /* FUNCTION */

    function close() {
      open = !open;
      settingsDiv.style.display = "none";
      openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "0";
      settingsDiv.style.display = "none";
    }

    function checkWidthToAppend(widthNum, parent1, parent2, children) {
      if (nowWidthLogin < widthNum) {
          if(parent1) {
              parent1.appendChild(children);
          } else {
              return;
          }
      } else {
          if(parent2) {
              parent2.appendChild(children);
          } else {
              return;
          }
      }

      window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
        // viewport and full window dimensions will change

        var width = window.innerWidth;

        if (width < 992) {
          parent1.appendChild(children);
        } else {
          parent2.appendChild(children);
        }
      });
    }

    function checkWidthToIconUser(widthNum, element) {
      if (nowWidthLogin < widthNum) {
        element.innerHTML =
          '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="font-size:18px !important" width="18" height="18" fill="white" class="bi bi-person" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path d="M8 8a3 3 0 1 0 0-6 3 3 0 0 0 0 6zm2-3a2 2 0 1 1-4 0 2 2 0 0 1 4 0zm4 8c0 1-1 1-1 1H3s-1 0-1-1 1-4 6-4 6 3 6 4zm-1-.004c-.001-.246-.154-.986-.832-1.664C11.516 10.68 10.289 10 8 10c-2.29 0-3.516.68-4.168 1.332-.678.678-.83 1.418-.832 1.664h10z"/>';
      } else {
        element.innerHTML =
          '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="font-size:18px !important" width="18" height="18" fill="black" class="bi bi-person" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path d="M8 8a3 3 0 1 0 0-6 3 3 0 0 0 0 6zm2-3a2 2 0 1 1-4 0 2 2 0 0 1 4 0zm4 8c0 1-1 1-1 1H3s-1 0-1-1 1-4 6-4 6 3 6 4zm-1-.004c-.001-.246-.154-.986-.832-1.664C11.516 10.68 10.289 10 8 10c-2.29 0-3.516.68-4.168 1.332-.678.678-.83 1.418-.832 1.664h10z"/>';
      }

      window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
        // viewport and full window dimensions will change

        var width = window.innerWidth;

        if (width < widthNum) {
          element.innerHTML =
            '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="font-size:18px !important" width="18" height="18" fill="white" class="bi bi-person" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path d="M8 8a3 3 0 1 0 0-6 3 3 0 0 0 0 6zm2-3a2 2 0 1 1-4 0 2 2 0 0 1 4 0zm4 8c0 1-1 1-1 1H3s-1 0-1-1 1-4 6-4 6 3 6 4zm-1-.004c-.001-.246-.154-.986-.832-1.664C11.516 10.68 10.289 10 8 10c-2.29 0-3.516.68-4.168 1.332-.678.678-.83 1.418-.832 1.664h10z"/>';
        } else {
          element.innerHTML =
            '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="font-size:18px !important" width="18" height="18" fill="black" class="bi bi-person" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path d="M8 8a3 3 0 1 0 0-6 3 3 0 0 0 0 6zm2-3a2 2 0 1 1-4 0 2 2 0 0 1 4 0zm4 8c0 1-1 1-1 1H3s-1 0-1-1 1-4 6-4 6 3 6 4zm-1-.004c-.001-.246-.154-.986-.832-1.664C11.516 10.68 10.289 10 8 10c-2.29 0-3.516.68-4.168 1.332-.678.678-.83 1.418-.832 1.664h10z"/>';
        }
      });
    }

    function checkWidthToIconArrow(widthNum, element) {
      if (nowWidthLogin < widthNum) {
        element.innerHTML =
          '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="12" height="15" fill="white" class="bi bi-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1.646 4.646a.5.5 0 0 1 .708 0L8 10.293l5.646-5.647a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708l-6 6a.5.5 0 0 1-.708 0l-6-6a.5.5 0 0 1 0-.708z"/>';
      } else {
        element.innerHTML =
          '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="12" height="15" fill="black" class="bi bi-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1.646 4.646a.5.5 0 0 1 .708 0L8 10.293l5.646-5.647a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708l-6 6a.5.5 0 0 1-.708 0l-6-6a.5.5 0 0 1 0-.708z"/>';
      }

      window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
        // viewport and full window dimensions will change

        var width = window.innerWidth;

        if (width < widthNum) {
          element.innerHTML =
            '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="12" height="15" fill="white" class="bi bi-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1.646 4.646a.5.5 0 0 1 .708 0L8 10.293l5.646-5.647a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708l-6 6a.5.5 0 0 1-.708 0l-6-6a.5.5 0 0 1 0-.708z"/>';
        } else {
          element.innerHTML =
            '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="12" height="15" fill="black" class="bi bi-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1.646 4.646a.5.5 0 0 1 .708 0L8 10.293l5.646-5.647a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708l-6 6a.5.5 0 0 1-.708 0l-6-6a.5.5 0 0 1 0-.708z"/>';
        }
      });
    }

    function mouseOver() {
      openSettingsContainerDiv.style.height = "90px";
      settingsDiv.style.display = "block";
      accountContainerDiv.style.backgroundColor = "black";
      formattedNameP.style.setProperty("color", "white", "important");
      accountIconUserDiv.innerHTML =

 document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  // --- Mobile-only move + The Latest heading fix ---
  const isMobile = window.matchMedia("(max-width: 768px)").matches;
  if (isMobile) {
    // 1) Move JW section
    const targetRegion = document.getElementById("tncms-region-front-one-top");
    const jwRegion = document.getElementById("tncms-region-front-full-two-top");

    if (targetRegion && jwRegion) {
      targetRegion.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", jwRegion);
      console.log("&#9989; Moved #tncms-region-front-full-two-top after #tncms-region-front-one-top");
    }

    // 2) Update "The Latest" block
    const latest = document.querySelector(".block-title.title-1505803");
    if (latest) {
      // Replace h4 with h3
      const h4 = latest.querySelector("h4");
      if (h4) {
        const h3 = document.createElement("h3");
        h3.textContent = h4.textContent.trim();
        h4.replaceWith(h3);
      }

      // Ensure .block-title-inner exists and contains the heading
      let inner = latest.querySelector(".block-title-inner");
      if (!inner) {
        inner = document.createElement("div");
        inner.className = "block-title-inner";
        latest.appendChild(inner);
      }
      const h3 = latest.querySelector("h3");
      if (h3 && h3.parentElement !== inner) inner.appendChild(h3);

      // Add mobile-only ::after underline
      const style = document.createElement("style");
      style.textContent = `
        @media (max-width: 768px) {
          .block-title.title-1505803 .block-title-inner::after {
            width: 7rem;

        <div class="card-headline"><h4 class="tnt-headline ">
        
             <a href="/news/business/vacant-downtown-new-orleans-storefront-grants/article_3d882922-85d9-4cb1-9af4-c696f2968c46.html#tncms-source=business-featured" class="tnt-asset-link" aria-label="Want to open a business in downtown New Orleans? A new program is offering cash to help.">
        

        
            Want to open a business in downtown New Orleans? A new program is offering cash to help.</a></h4></div>
    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                        
                        
                            <div class="card-lead">
                                <p class="tnt-summary">Business owners looking to lease retail space in downtown New Orleans could get a boost from a pilot program aimed at helping to cover the cost of renovating long-vacant storefronts. </p>
                            </div>

            Gov. Jeff Landry cheers Meta expansion as local leaders, residents react</a></h4></div>
    
                    
                    
                    
                    
                        
                        
                            <div class="card-lead">
                                <p class="tnt-summary">Gov.     <script>
        __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
        });
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-event]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.tncmsTrackEvent));
            });
        });

                var dmpData = el.dataset.tncmsTrackDmp;

        });

<script>/*<![CDATA[*/ 
                __tnt.googleEvent = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.trigger',
                             'tncms.event.trigger.category': obj.category,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.action': obj.action,
                             'tncms.event.trigger.label': obj.label, 
                             'tncms.event.trigger.value': obj.value
                    });
                }
                /* Virtual page view */
                __tnt.googlePageView = function(obj) {
                    var sURL = obj.url.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '');
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.virtual_pageview',
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.url': sURL,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.title': obj.title,
                            'tncms.event.virtual_pageview.metric': obj.metric
                    });
                }
                /* Social event */
                __tnt.googleSocial = function(obj) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'tncms.event.social',
                            'tncms.event.social.network': obj.network,
                            'tncms.event.social.action': obj.socialAction,
                            'tncms.event.social.target': obj.url
                    });
                } /*]]>*/</script>
